Evaluating LLM Safety Under Repeated Inference via Accelerated Prompt Stress Testing
Authors: Keita Broadwater
First: 2026-02-12T10:09:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-28T16:38:37+00:00
Comments: 23 pages, 9 figures; editorial and LaTeX revisions for clarity; improved presentation of methodology and results; updated figures, tables, and float placement; clarified temperature sensitivity and deployment-risk analysis; expanded reporting from the same experiments; results unchanged in substance
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Traditional benchmarks for large language models (LLMs), such as HELM and AIR-BENCH, primarily assess safety through breadth-oriented evaluation across diverse tasks and risk categories. However, real-world deployment often exposes a different class of risk: operational failures that arise under repeated inference on identical or near-identical prompts rather than from broad task-level underperformance. In high-stakes settings, response consistency and safety under sustained use are therefore critical. We introduce Accelerated Prompt Stress Testing (APST), a depth-oriented evaluation framework inspired by highly accelerated stress testing in reliability engineering. APST repeatedly samples identical prompts under controlled operational conditions (such as decoding temperature) to surface latent failure modes including hallucinations, refusal inconsistency, and unsafe completions. Rather than treating failures as isolated events, APST models them as stochastic outcomes of repeated inference and uses Bernoulli and binomial formulations to estimate per-inference failure probabilities. Applying APST to multiple instruction-tuned LLMs evaluated on AIR-BENCH 2024--derived safety and security prompts, we find that models with comparable shallow-evaluation scores can exhibit substantially different empirical failure rates under repeated sampling. These results show that single-sample or low-depth evaluation can obscure meaningful differences in deployment-relevant reliability. APST complements existing benchmark methodologies by providing a practical framework for estimating failure frequency under sustained use and comparing safety reliability across models and decoding configurations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过加速提示压力测试评估大语言模型的安全性
传统的大语言模型（LLMs）基准，如HELM和AIR-BENCH，主要通过在多样任务和风险类别中的广度评估来评估安全性。然而，实际部署往往暴露出另一类风险：在相同或近似相同的提示下重复推理所导致的操作失败，而不是广泛任务级别的表现不佳。在高风险环境中，响应一致性和持续使用下的安全性至关重要。我们引入了加速提示压力测试（APST），这是一种受可靠性工程中高度加速压力测试启发的深度评估框架。APST在受控操作条件下（如解码温度）重复采样相同的提示，以揭示潜在的失败模式，包括幻觉、拒绝不一致和不安全的完成。APST将失败视为重复推理的随机结果，而不是孤立事件，并使用伯努利和二项式公式来估计每次推理的失败概率。将APST应用于多个在AIR-BENCH 2024上评估的指令调优LLMs的安全和安全提示，我们发现具有可比浅层评估分数的模型在重复采样下可能表现出显著不同的经验失败率。这些结果表明，单样本或低深度评估可能掩盖在部署相关可靠性方面的有意义差异。APST通过提供一个实用框架来估计持续使用下的失败频率，并比较模型和解码配置之间的安全可靠性，补充了现有的基准方法。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the limitations of traditional benchmarks for evaluating large language models (LLMs), which often focus on broad task performance and overlook operational risks associated with repeated inference on similar prompts. Existing methods fail to capture the nuances of response consistency and safety in real-world applications, particularly in high-stakes environments. The proposed Accelerated Prompt Stress Testing (APST) framework offers a depth-oriented evaluation approach that systematically samples identical prompts under controlled conditions to identify latent failure modes such as hallucinations and unsafe completions. By modeling failures as stochastic outcomes and employing Bernoulli and binomial formulations, APST provides a more accurate estimation of failure probabilities during repeated use. The application of APST to various instruction-tuned LLMs reveals significant discrepancies in empirical failure rates, highlighting that traditional shallow evaluations can mask critical differences in reliability. This methodology enhances existing benchmarks by offering a practical means to assess and compare safety reliability across models and configurations under sustained use.
本文探讨了传统的大型语言模型（LLM）评估基准的局限性，这些基准主要关注广泛的任务表现，往往忽视在相似提示下重复推理时发生的操作失败。以往的方法未能捕捉高风险环境中响应一致性和安全性的细微差别，因此作者提出了加速提示压力测试（APST），这是一种深度导向的评估框架，通过模拟对相同提示的重复采样来识别潜在的失败模式。本文的贡献在于引入了一种系统的方法，将模型失败视为随机结果，利用伯努利和二项分布公式估计重复推理过程中的失败概率。该方法应用于多个指令调优的LLM，揭示了具有相似浅层评估分数的模型在重复测试下可能具有显著不同的失败率，从而强调了深度导向评估在评估模型在实际应用中可靠性和安全性的重要性。
Adaptive Prompt Embedding Optimization for LLM Jailbreaking
Authors: Miles Q. Li, Benjamin C. M. Fung, Boyang Li, Radin Hamidi Rad, Ebrahim Bagheri
First: 2026-04-27T20:39:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-27T20:39:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Existing white-box jailbreak attacks against aligned LLMs typically append discrete adversarial suffixes to the user prompt, which visibly alters the prompt and operates in a combinatorial token space. Prior work has avoided directly optimizing the embeddings of the original prompt tokens, presumably because perturbing them risks destroying the prompt's semantic content. We propose Prompt Embedding Optimization (PEO), a multi-round white-box jailbreak that directly optimizes the embeddings of the original prompt tokens without appending any adversarial tokens, and show that the concern is unfounded: the optimized embeddings remain close enough to their originals that the visible prompt string is preserved exactly after nearest-token projection, and quantitative analysis shows the model's responses stay on topic for the large majority of prompts. PEO combines continuous embedding-space optimization with structured continuation targets and an adaptive failure-focused schedule. Counterintuitively, later PEO rounds can benefit from heuristic composite response scaffolds that are not natural standalone templates, yet ASR-Judge shows that the resulting gains are not merely empty formatting or scaffold-only outputs. Across two standard harmful-behavior benchmarks and competing white-box attacks spanning discrete suffix search, appended adversarial embeddings, and search-based adversarial generation, PEO outperforms all of them in our experiments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：用于大型语言模型越狱的自适应提示嵌入优化
现有针对对齐大型语言模型的白盒越狱攻击通常在用户提示后附加离散的对抗后缀，这明显改变了提示并在组合标记空间中操作。之前的工作避免直接优化原始提示标记的嵌入，可能是因为扰动它们会破坏提示的语义内容。我们提出了提示嵌入优化（PEO），这是一种多轮白盒越狱，直接优化原始提示标记的嵌入，而不附加任何对抗标记，并表明这种担忧是没有根据的：优化后的嵌入与原始嵌入保持足够接近，以至于在最近标记投影后可见的提示字符串完全保留，定量分析表明模型的响应在绝大多数提示中保持主题一致。PEO结合了连续嵌入空间优化、结构化延续目标和自适应失败聚焦调度。出乎意料的是，后期PEO轮次可以受益于并非自然独立模板的启发式复合响应支架，但ASR-Judge显示，所产生的收益不仅仅是空的格式或仅支架输出。在两个标准有害行为基准和竞争白盒攻击（包括离散后缀搜索、附加对抗嵌入和基于搜索的对抗生成）中，PEO在我们的实验中表现优于所有这些方法。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the limitations of existing white-box jailbreak attacks on aligned large language models (LLMs), which typically modify user prompts by appending discrete adversarial suffixes, leading to visible alterations and operating in a combinatorial token space. Previous methods have refrained from optimizing the embeddings of original prompt tokens due to concerns about losing semantic integrity, but this paper introduces Prompt Embedding Optimization (PEO), a novel approach that directly optimizes these embeddings without adding adversarial tokens. PEO is well-motivated as it preserves the original prompt's visible string while ensuring the model's responses remain relevant. The methodology involves a multi-round optimization process that combines continuous embedding-space adjustments with structured continuation targets and an adaptive schedule focused on failure. The experimental results demonstrate that PEO significantly outperforms traditional methods across two harmful-behavior benchmarks and various competing white-box attacks, confirming its effectiveness in achieving the research goals.
本文针对现有的白盒监狱攻击方法的局限性进行了研究，这些方法通常通过附加离散的对抗后缀来修改用户提示，导致可见的变化并在组合标记空间中操作。以往的方法避免直接优化原始提示标记的嵌入，原因在于担心会损失语义完整性。提出的提示嵌入优化（PEO）方法创新性地直接优化这些嵌入，保持了原始提示的可见性和语义内容，从而克服了以往方法的局限性。本文的贡献在于证明优化后的嵌入能够有效保持提示的完整性，同时增强模型的响应能力。该方法论涉及一个多轮优化过程，结合了连续嵌入空间优化、结构化延续目标和自适应失败聚焦调度。结果表明，PEO在两个有害行为基准和多种竞争的白盒攻击中显著优于现有方法，取得了支持有效监狱攻击目标的卓越性能。
Beyond Context: Large Language Models' Failure to Grasp Users' Intent
Authors: Ahmed M. Hussain, Salahuddin Salahuddin
First: 2025-12-24T11:15:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-24T20:27:34+00:00
Comments: 22 pages and 23 figures; updated authors list and revised manuscript
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Current Large Language Models (LLMs) safety approaches focus on explicitly harmful content while overlooking a critical vulnerability: the inability to understand context and recognize user intent. This creates exploitable vulnerabilities that malicious users can systematically leverage to circumvent safety mechanisms. We empirically evaluate multiple state-of-the-art LLMs, including ChatGPT, Claude, Gemini, and DeepSeek. Our analysis demonstrates the circumvention of reliable safety mechanisms through emotional framing, progressive revelation, and academic justification techniques. Notably, reasoning-enabled configurations amplified rather than mitigated the effectiveness of exploitation, increasing factual precision while failing to interrogate the underlying intent. The exception was Claude Opus 4.1, which prioritized intent detection over information provision in some use cases. This pattern reveals that current architectural designs create systematic vulnerabilities. These limitations require paradigmatic shifts toward contextual understanding and intent recognition as core safety capabilities rather than post-hoc protective mechanisms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越上下文：大型语言模型未能理解用户意图
当前大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全方法专注于显性有害内容，而忽视了一个关键漏洞：无法理解上下文和识别用户意图。这导致了恶意用户可以系统性利用的可利用漏洞，从而规避安全机制。我们对多个最先进的LLMs进行了实证评估，包括ChatGPT、Claude、Gemini和DeepSeek。我们的分析表明，通过情感框架、渐进揭示和学术辩护技术，可靠安全机制被规避。值得注意的是，启用推理的配置增强了而不是减轻了利用的有效性，提高了事实精确性，但未能质疑潜在意图。例外是Claude Opus 4.1，在某些用例中优先考虑意图检测而非信息提供。这一模式揭示了当前架构设计造成的系统性漏洞。这些局限性需要在上下文理解和意图识别方面进行范式转变，将其作为核心安全能力，而不是事后保护机制。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the limitations of current Large Language Models (LLMs) in understanding user intent and context, which exposes them to exploitation by malicious users. Previous methods primarily focused on filtering harmful content but failed to recognize the nuances of user intent, leading to vulnerabilities in safety mechanisms. This paper proposes a shift towards integrating contextual understanding and intent recognition as fundamental safety features, rather than relying on reactive measures. The methodology involves empirical evaluations of state-of-the-art LLMs, revealing that techniques like emotional framing and progressive revelation can bypass safety protocols, with only Claude Opus 4.1 showing some effectiveness in intent detection. The findings indicate that existing architectural designs are inadequate, necessitating a rethinking of safety approaches to enhance model robustness against exploitation.
本研究关注当前大型语言模型（LLMs）在理解用户意图和上下文方面的局限性，这导致了可被恶意用户利用的漏洞，从而绕过安全机制。以往的方法主要集中在过滤有害内容，但未能考虑用户意图的细微差别，导致LLM安全性存在系统性弱点。本文提出将上下文理解和意图识别作为基本安全特性，而不仅仅是反应性措施的转变。研究方法包括对多种先进LLM的实证评估，揭示情感框架和渐进揭示等技术可能削弱安全协议，而Claude Opus 4.1则通过强调意图检测成为一个例外。研究结果表明，现有的架构设计不足以确保用户安全，强调了LLM开发中需要进行范式转变的必要性。
Logic Jailbreak: Efficiently Unlocking LLM Safety Restrictions Through Formal Logical Expression
Authors: Jingyu Peng, Maolin Wang, Nan Wang, Jiatong Li, Yuchen Li, Yuyang Ye, Wanyu Wang, Pengyue Jia, Kai Zhang, Xiangyu Zhao
First: 2025-05-18T04:23:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-24T07:04:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite substantial advancements in aligning large language models (LLMs) with human values, current safety mechanisms remain susceptible to jailbreak attacks. We hypothesize that this vulnerability stems from distributional discrepancies between alignment-oriented prompts and malicious prompts. To investigate this, we introduce LogiBreak, a novel and universal black-box jailbreak method that leverages logical expression translation to circumvent LLM safety systems. By converting harmful natural language prompts into formal logical expressions, LogiBreak exploits the distributional gap between alignment data and logic-based inputs, preserving the underlying semantic intent and readability while evading safety constraints. We evaluate LogiBreak on a multilingual jailbreak dataset spanning three languages, demonstrating its effectiveness across various evaluation settings and linguistic contexts.
中文标题/摘要
标题：逻辑越狱：通过形式逻辑表达高效解锁大型语言模型安全限制
尽管在将大型语言模型（LLMs）与人类价值观对齐方面取得了重大进展，但当前的安全机制仍然容易受到越狱攻击。我们假设这种脆弱性源于对齐导向提示与恶意提示之间的分布差异。为此，我们引入了LogiBreak，这是一种新颖且通用的黑箱越狱方法，利用逻辑表达翻译来规避LLM安全系统。通过将有害的自然语言提示转换为形式逻辑表达，LogiBreak利用对齐数据与基于逻辑的输入之间的分布差距，保持潜在的语义意图和可读性，同时规避安全约束。我们在涵盖三种语言的多语言越狱数据集上评估LogiBreak，展示了其在各种评估设置和语言环境中的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the ongoing challenge of jailbreak attacks on large language models (LLMs), which remain vulnerable despite advancements in aligning them with human values. Previous methods have struggled with distributional discrepancies between alignment-oriented and malicious prompts, leading to ineffective safety mechanisms. The proposed approach, LogiBreak, introduces a novel black-box method that translates harmful natural language prompts into formal logical expressions, effectively exploiting the distributional gap while maintaining semantic intent and readability. This method is well-motivated as it directly targets the identified vulnerabilities in existing safety systems. The paper contributes by demonstrating LogiBreak's effectiveness on a multilingual jailbreak dataset across three languages, achieving significant performance improvements in various evaluation settings and supporting the goal of enhancing LLM safety.

Toward Principled LLM Safety Testing: Solving the Jailbreak Oracle Problem
Authors: Shuyi Lin, Anshuman Suri, Alina Oprea, Cheng Tan
First: 2025-06-17T20:37:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-24T04:36:54+00:00
Comments: Accepted to MLSys 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
As large language models (LLMs) become increasingly deployed in safety-critical applications, the lack of systematic methods to assess their vulnerability to jailbreak attacks presents a critical security gap. We introduce the jailbreak oracle problem: given a model, prompt, and decoding strategy, determine whether a jailbreak response can be generated with likelihood exceeding a specified threshold. This formalization enables a principled study of jailbreak vulnerabilities. Answering the jailbreak oracle problem poses significant computational challenges, as the search space grows exponentially with response length. We present Boa, the first system designed for efficiently solving the jailbreak oracle problem. Boa employs a two-phase search strategy: (1) breadth-first sampling to identify easily accessible jailbreaks, followed by (2) depth-first priority search guided by fine-grained safety scores to systematically explore promising yet low-probability paths. Boa enables rigorous security assessments including systematic defense evaluation, standardized comparison of red team attacks, and model certification under extreme adversarial conditions. Code is available at https://github.com/shuyilinn/BOA/tree/mlsys2026ae
中文标题/摘要
标题：朝着原则性的大型语言模型安全测试：解决越狱预言机问题
随着大型语言模型（LLMs）在安全关键应用中的日益部署，缺乏系统的方法来评估它们对越狱攻击的脆弱性，形成了一个关键的安全缺口。我们引入了越狱预言机问题：给定一个模型、提示和解码策略，确定是否可以生成一个越狱响应，其概率超过指定阈值。这个形式化使得对越狱脆弱性的原则性研究成为可能。回答越狱预言机问题面临显著的计算挑战，因为搜索空间随着响应长度的增加而呈指数增长。我们提出了Boa，这是第一个旨在高效解决越狱预言机问题的系统。Boa采用两阶段搜索策略：（1）广度优先采样以识别易于访问的越狱，随后（2）深度优先优先搜索，通过细粒度安全评分引导，系统地探索有前景但概率较低的路径。Boa使得严格的安全评估成为可能，包括系统的防御评估、红队攻击的标准化比较，以及在极端对抗条件下的模型认证。代码可在 https://github.com/shuyilinn/BOA/tree/mlsys2026ae 获取。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the critical security gap in assessing the vulnerability of large language models (LLMs) to jailbreak attacks, a concern as these models are increasingly used in safety-critical applications. Previous methods lacked systematic approaches to evaluate such vulnerabilities, leading to insufficient security assessments. The proposed method, Boa, differs by introducing a formalized jailbreak oracle problem and employing a two-phase search strategy that combines breadth-first sampling and depth-first priority search, effectively tackling the computational challenges associated with the exponential growth of the search space. This paper contributes by enabling rigorous security assessments, including defense evaluations and model certifications under adversarial conditions. Boa has demonstrated its effectiveness in systematically identifying jailbreak responses, thereby supporting the goal of enhancing LLM safety testing.
本研究解决了在安全关键应用中评估大型语言模型（LLMs）对越狱攻击脆弱性的关键安全缺口。以往的方法缺乏系统性评估此类脆弱性的手段，导致在确定越狱响应的可能性时面临重大挑战。所提出的方法Boa通过引入正式的越狱oracle问题，并采用结合广度优先采样和深度优先优先搜索的两阶段搜索策略，解决了与搜索空间指数增长相关的计算挑战。本文的贡献在于提供了一种新颖的系统，用于严格的安全评估，能够进行系统的防御评估和攻击的标准化比较。Boa的性能使其能够有效地在极端对抗条件下进行模型认证，支持增强LLM安全测试的目标。
AISafetyBenchExplorer: A Metric-Aware Catalogue of AI Safety Benchmarks Reveals Fragmented Measurement and Weak Benchmark Governance
Authors: Abiodun A. Solanke
First: 2026-04-14T15:26:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-23T13:27:05+00:00
Comments: This paper has been withdrawn by the author while an institutional affiliation compliance matter is under review. It may be resubmitted once the matter is resolved
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid expansion of large language model (LLM) safety evaluation has produced a substantial benchmark ecosystem, but not a correspondingly coherent measurement ecosystem. We present AISafetyBenchExplorer, a structured catalogue of 195 AI safety benchmarks released between 2018 and 2026, organized through a multi-sheet schema that records benchmark-level metadata, metric-level definitions, benchmark-paper metadata, and repository activity. This design enables meta-analysis not only of what benchmarks exist, but also of how safety is operationalized, aggregated, and judged across the literature. Using the updated catalogue, we identify a central structural problem: benchmark proliferation has outpaced measurement standardization. The current landscape is dominated by medium-complexity benchmarks (94/195), while only 7 benchmarks occupy the Popular tier. The workbook further reports strong concentration around English-only evaluation (165/195), evaluation-only resources (170/195), stale GitHub repositories (137/195), stale Hugging Face datasets (96/195), and heavy reliance on arXiv preprints among benchmarks with known venue metadata. At the metric level, the catalogue shows that familiar labels such as accuracy, F1 score, safety score, and aggregate benchmark scores often conceal materially different judges, aggregation rules, and threat models. We argue that the field's main failure mode is fragmentation rather than scarcity. Researchers now have many benchmark artifacts, but they often lack a shared measurement language, a principled basis for benchmark selection, and durable stewardship norms for post publication maintenance. AISafetyBenchExplorer addresses this gap by providing a traceable benchmark catalogue, a controlled metadata schema, and a complexity taxonomy that together support more rigorous benchmark discovery, comparison, and meta-evaluation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AISafetyBenchExplorer：一个关注度量的AI安全基准目录揭示了分散的测量和薄弱的基准治理
大型语言模型（LLM）安全评估的快速扩展产生了一个庞大的基准生态系统，但没有相应连贯的测量生态系统。我们提出了AISafetyBenchExplorer，这是一个结构化的目录，包含2018年至2026年间发布的195个AI安全基准，采用多表格模式记录基准级元数据、度量级定义、基准论文元数据和存储库活动。该设计不仅支持对现有基准的元分析，还支持对安全如何在文献中被操作、聚合和评判的分析。使用更新的目录，我们识别出一个核心结构性问题：基准的激增超过了测量的标准化。目前的格局以中等复杂度的基准为主（94/195），而只有7个基准位于流行层级。工作簿进一步报告了对仅英语评估（165/195）、仅评估资源（170/195）、过时的GitHub存储库（137/195）、过时的Hugging Face数据集（96/195）以及在已知场地元数据的基准中对arXiv预印本的高度依赖的强烈集中。在度量层面，目录显示，熟悉的标签如准确率、F1分数、安全分数和聚合基准分数常常掩盖了实质上不同的评判者、聚合规则和威胁模型。我们认为，该领域的主要失败模式是碎片化而非稀缺。研究人员现在拥有许多基准文献，但通常缺乏共享的测量语言、基准选择的原则基础以及发布后维护的持久管理规范。AISafetyBenchExplorer通过提供可追溯的基准目录、受控的元数据模式和复杂性分类法来填补这一空白，从而支持更严格的基准发现、比较和元评估。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the fragmented landscape of AI safety benchmarks that has emerged alongside the rapid growth of large language model safety evaluations. Previous methods have resulted in a proliferation of benchmarks without a coherent measurement framework, leading to issues such as a lack of standardization and heavy reliance on English-only evaluations. The proposed AISafetyBenchExplorer offers a structured catalogue of 195 AI safety benchmarks, organized through a multi-sheet schema that captures detailed metadata and enables meta-analysis of benchmark effectiveness and operationalization of safety. This approach contributes to the field by providing a traceable benchmark catalogue and a complexity taxonomy, facilitating better benchmark discovery and comparison. The methodology allows for a comprehensive overview of existing benchmarks, revealing that the majority are medium-complexity and highlighting the need for improved measurement standards, thereby supporting the goal of establishing a more unified measurement language in AI safety evaluation.
本研究解决了随着大型语言模型安全评估快速增长而出现的AI安全基准的碎片化问题。以往的方法导致基准的数量激增，但缺乏一致的测量框架，造成标准化不足和对仅使用英语的评估的高度依赖。提出的AISafetyBenchExplorer提供了一个结构化的195个AI安全基准的目录，采用多表格架构捕捉详细的元数据，并支持基准和指标的元分析。这种方法旨在统一测量语言并改善基准治理，为该领域提供更严格的评估实践。该方法包括复杂性分类法和受控元数据架构，促进了基准的更好发现和比较，最终提升了不同基准的安全评估质量。
Secure LLM Fine-Tuning via Safety-Aware Probing
Authors: Chengcan Wu, Zhixin Zhang, Zeming Wei, Yihao Zhang, Xiaokun Luan, Meng Sun
First: 2025-05-22T14:52:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-23T08:31:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) have achieved remarkable success across many applications, but their ability to generate harmful content raises serious safety concerns. Although safety alignment techniques are often applied during pre-training or post-training, recent studies show that subsequent fine-tuning on adversarial or even benign data can still compromise model safety. In this paper, we revisit the fundamental question of why fine-tuning on non-harmful data may nevertheless degrade safety. We show that the safety and task-performance loss landscapes are partially decoupled, so updates that improve task-specific performance may still move the model toward unsafe regions. Based on this insight, we propose a safety-aware probing (SAP) optimization framework for mitigating safety risks during fine-tuning. Concretely, SAP uses contrastive safety signals to locate safety-correlated directions, and optimizes a lightweight probe that perturbs hidden-state propagation during fine-tuning, thereby steering parameter updates away from harmful trajectories while preserving task-specific learning. Extensive experiments show that SAP consistently improves the safety--utility tradeoff across multiple models and tasks. Averaged over multiple LLMs, SAP reduces the harmful score significantly relative to standard fine-tuning, outperforming strong baselines while maintaining competitive task-specific performance. SAP also demonstrates stronger robustness under harmful data poisoning, adversarial fine-tuning, and a dedicated post-fine-tuning adaptive attack, validating that SAP is an effective and scalable framework for preserving LLM safety during fine-tuning. Our code is available at https://github.com/ChengcanWu/SAP.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过安全感知探测进行安全的LLM微调
大型语言模型（LLMs）在许多应用中取得了显著成功，但其生成有害内容的能力引发了严重的安全担忧。尽管安全对齐技术通常在预训练或后训练期间应用，但最近的研究表明，随后在对抗性或甚至良性数据上的微调仍然可能危及模型安全。本文重新审视了一个基本问题，即为什么在无害数据上的微调仍可能降低安全性。我们表明，安全性和任务性能损失的景观部分解耦，因此改善任务特定性能的更新可能仍会将模型推向不安全区域。基于这一见解，我们提出了一种安全感知探测（SAP）优化框架，以减轻微调过程中的安全风险。具体而言，SAP使用对比安全信号来定位与安全相关的方向，并优化一个轻量级探测器，在微调过程中扰动隐藏状态传播，从而将参数更新引导远离有害轨迹，同时保持任务特定学习。大量实验表明，SAP在多个模型和任务中始终改善安全性与效用的权衡。在多个LLM上平均，SAP相对于标准微调显著降低了有害评分，超越了强基线，同时保持了竞争性的任务特定性能。SAP在有害数据中毒、对抗性微调和专门的后微调自适应攻击下也表现出更强的鲁棒性，验证了SAP是一个有效且可扩展的框架，用于在微调过程中保持LLM的安全性。我们的代码可在https://github.com/ChengcanWu/SAP获取。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the safety concerns associated with large language models (LLMs), particularly how fine-tuning on non-harmful data can still lead to safety degradation. Previous methods focused on safety alignment during pre-training or post-training but failed to prevent safety risks during fine-tuning, as improvements in task performance could inadvertently push models toward unsafe regions. This paper introduces a safety-aware probing (SAP) optimization framework that utilizes contrastive safety signals to guide parameter updates away from harmful trajectories while still enabling effective task-specific learning. The methodology involves optimizing a lightweight probe that perturbs hidden-state propagation during fine-tuning. Experimental results demonstrate that SAP significantly reduces harmful scores compared to standard fine-tuning across various models and tasks, while maintaining competitive task-specific performance and showing enhanced robustness against harmful data poisoning and adversarial attacks, thus confirming its effectiveness in preserving LLM safety during fine-tuning.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLMs）所面临的安全问题，特别是如何在非有害数据上进行微调仍可能导致安全性下降。以往的方法主要集中在预训练或后训练期间的安全对齐，但未能考虑微调过程中安全性与任务性能的解耦，这可能会无意中将模型推向不安全的区域。提出的安全感知探测（SAP）框架引入了一种新颖的优化方法，利用对比安全信号引导参数更新远离有害轨迹，同时实现任务特定学习。通过广泛的实验验证，该方法显示SAP显著减少有害输出，同时在各种模型和任务中保持竞争性能，从而有效增强了LLM微调中的安全性与效用的权衡。
LASA: Language-Agnostic Semantic Alignment at the Semantic Bottleneck for LLM Safety
Authors: Junxiao Yang, Haoran Liu, Jinzhe Tu, Jiale Cheng, Zhexin Zhang, Shiyao Cui, Jiaqi Weng, Jialing Tao, Hui Xue, Hongning Wang, Han Qiu, Minlie Huang
First: 2026-04-13T15:59:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-23T04:47:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) often demonstrate strong safety performance in high-resource languages, yet exhibit severe vulnerabilities when queried in low-resource languages. We attribute this gap to a mismatch between language-agnostic semantic understanding ability and language-dominant safety alignment biased toward high-resource languages. Consistent with this hypothesis, we empirically identify the semantic bottleneck in LLMs, an intermediate layer in which the geometry of model representations is governed primarily by shared semantic content rather than language identity. Building on this observation, we propose Language-Agnostic Semantic Alignment (LASA), which anchors safety alignment directly in semantic bottlenecks. Experiments show that LASA substantially improves safety across all languages: average attack success rate (ASR) drops from 24.7% to 2.8% on LLaMA-3.1-8B-Instruct and remains around 3-4% across Qwen2.5 and Qwen3 Instruct models (7B-32B). Together, our analysis and method offer a representation-level perspective on LLM safety, suggesting that safety alignment requires anchoring safety understanding not in surface text, but in the model's language-agnostic semantic space.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LASA：在语义瓶颈处实现语言无关的语义对齐以提高大型语言模型的安全性
大型语言模型（LLMs）在高资源语言中通常表现出强大的安全性能，但在低资源语言中查询时却表现出严重的脆弱性。我们将这一差距归因于语言无关的语义理解能力与偏向高资源语言的语言主导安全对齐之间的不匹配。与这一假设一致，我们实证识别了LLMs中的语义瓶颈，这是一个中间层，其中模型表示的几何形状主要由共享的语义内容而非语言身份所主导。基于这一观察，我们提出了语言无关的语义对齐（LASA），直接在语义瓶颈中锚定安全对齐。实验表明，LASA显著提高了所有语言的安全性：在LLaMA-3.1-8B-Instruct上的平均攻击成功率（ASR）从24.7%降至2.8%，在Qwen2.5和Qwen3 Instruct模型（7B-32B）中保持在3-4%左右。我们的分析和方法共同提供了对LLM安全性的表示级别视角，表明安全对齐需要将安全理解锚定在模型的语言无关语义空间中，而非表面文本上。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the significant safety performance gap in large language models (LLMs) when operating in low-resource languages compared to high-resource languages, which is attributed to a mismatch between language-agnostic semantic understanding and language-dominant safety alignment. Previous methods have focused on surface text for safety alignment, leading to vulnerabilities in low-resource contexts. The proposed approach, Language-Agnostic Semantic Alignment (LASA), directly anchors safety alignment in the identified semantic bottleneck, where model representations are primarily influenced by shared semantic content rather than language identity. The contribution of this paper lies in providing a representation-level perspective on LLM safety, demonstrating that LASA significantly reduces the average attack success rate from 24.7% to 2.8% on LLaMA-3.1-8B-Instruct and maintains low rates around 3-4% across other models, effectively supporting the goal of enhancing safety across all languages.

Dialect vs Demographics: Quantifying LLM Bias from Implicit Linguistic Signals vs. Explicit User Profiles
Authors: Irti Haq, Belén Saldías
First: 2026-04-22T23:33:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T23:33:18+00:00
Comments: In The 2026 ACM Conference on Fairness, Accountability, and Transparency (FAccT '26), June 25--28, 2026, Montreal, Canada. ACM, New York, NY, USA, 32 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As state-of-the-art Large Language Models (LLMs) have become ubiquitous, ensuring equitable performance across diverse demographics is critical. However, it remains unclear whether these disparities arise from the explicitly stated identity itself or from the way identity is signaled. In real-world interactions, users' identity is often conveyed implicitly through a complex combination of various socio-linguistic factors. This study disentangles these signals by employing a factorial design with over 24,000 responses from two open-weight LLMs (Gemma-3-12B and Qwen-3-VL-8B), comparing prompts with explicitly announced user profiles against implicit dialect signals (e.g., AAVE, Singlish) across various sensitive domains. Our results uncover a unique paradox in LLM safety where users achieve ``better'' performance by sounding like a demographic than by stating they belong to it. Explicit identity prompts activate aggressive safety filters, increasing refusal rates and reducing semantic similarity compared to our reference text for Black users. In contrast, implicit dialect cues trigger a powerful ``dialect jailbreak,'' reducing refusal probability to near zero while simultaneously achieving a greater level of semantic similarity to the reference texts compared to Standard American English prompts. However, this ``dialect jailbreak'' introduces a critical safety trade-off regarding content sanitization. We find that current safety alignment techniques are brittle and over-indexed on explicit keywords, creating a bifurcated user experience where ``standard'' users receive cautious, sanitized information while dialect speakers navigate a less sanitized, more raw, and potentially a more hostile information landscape and highlights a fundamental tension in alignment--between equitable and linguistic diversity--and underscores the need for safety mechanisms that generalize beyond explicit cues.
中文标题/摘要
标题：方言与人口统计：量化隐性语言信号与显性用户档案中的LLM偏见
随着最先进的大型语言模型（LLMs）变得无处不在，确保在不同人口统计中公平的表现至关重要。然而，这些差异是否源于明确声明的身份本身，还是身份信号的方式仍不清楚。在现实世界的互动中，用户的身份通常通过各种社会语言因素的复杂组合隐性传达。本研究通过采用因子设计，分析来自两个开放权重LLM（Gemma-3-12B和Qwen-3-VL-8B）的超过24,000个响应，比较显性用户档案的提示与隐性方言信号（例如，AAVE，Singlish）在各种敏感领域的表现。我们的结果揭示了LLM安全性中的一个独特悖论，即用户通过听起来像某个群体而不是明确声明自己属于该群体来获得“更好”的表现。显性身份提示激活了激进的安全过滤器，增加了拒绝率，并减少了与黑人用户参考文本的语义相似性。相比之下，隐性方言线索触发了强大的“方言越狱”，将拒绝概率降低到接近零，同时在与标准美式英语提示相比时，达到更高的语义相似性。然而，这种“方言越狱”引入了关于内容净化的关键安全权衡。我们发现当前的安全对齐技术脆弱，并过度依赖显性关键词，造成了“标准”用户获得谨慎、净化的信息，而方言使用者则在一个较少净化、更原始且可能更具敌意的信息环境中导航，突显了对齐中的基本紧张关系——在公平性与语言多样性之间，并强调了需要超越显性线索的安全机制。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the critical issue of equitable performance in Large Language Models (LLMs) across diverse demographics, focusing on whether disparities stem from explicit identity statements or implicit linguistic signals. Previous methods have primarily relied on explicit user profiles, which can trigger aggressive safety filters and lead to poorer performance for certain demographic groups. The proposed approach employs a factorial design analyzing over 24,000 responses from two LLMs, comparing explicit prompts against implicit dialect signals, revealing that users often achieve better outcomes by using dialect cues rather than stating their identity. This study contributes to understanding the safety trade-offs in LLMs, demonstrating that implicit signals can reduce refusal rates and enhance semantic similarity, while also highlighting the limitations of current safety alignment techniques that favor explicit cues. The findings indicate a need for improved safety mechanisms that accommodate linguistic diversity without compromising user experience.

LLM Safety From Within: Detecting Harmful Content with Internal Representations
Authors: Difan Jiao, Yilun Liu, Ye Yuan, Zhenwei Tang, Linfeng Du, Haolun Wu, Ashton Anderson
First: 2026-04-20T17:17:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T17:17:07+00:00
Comments: 17 pages,10 figures,6 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Guard models are widely used to detect harmful content in user prompts and LLM responses. However, state-of-the-art guard models rely solely on terminal-layer representations and overlook the rich safety-relevant features distributed across internal layers. We present SIREN, a lightweight guard model that harnesses these internal features. By identifying safety neurons via linear probing and combining them through an adaptive layer-weighted strategy, SIREN builds a harmfulness detector from LLM internals without modifying the underlying model. Our comprehensive evaluation shows that SIREN substantially outperforms state-of-the-art open-source guard models across multiple benchmarks while using 250 times fewer trainable parameters. Moreover, SIREN exhibits superior generalization to unseen benchmarks, naturally enables real-time streaming detection, and significantly improves inference efficiency compared to generative guard models. Overall, our results highlight LLM internal states as a promising foundation for practical, high-performance harmfulness detection.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从内部保障LLM安全：利用内部表示检测有害内容
保护模型广泛用于检测用户提示和LLM响应中的有害内容。然而，最先进的保护模型仅依赖于终层表示，忽视了分布在内部层中的丰富安全相关特征。我们提出了SIREN，这是一种轻量级保护模型，利用这些内部特征。通过线性探测识别安全神经元，并通过自适应层加权策略将其结合，SIREN在不修改基础模型的情况下，从LLM内部构建有害性检测器。我们的综合评估表明，SIREN在多个基准测试中显著优于最先进的开源保护模型，同时使用的可训练参数少达250倍。此外，SIREN在未见基准上的泛化能力更强，自然实现实时流检测，并显著提高了推理效率，相较于生成性保护模型。总体而言，我们的结果强调LLM内部状态作为实用高性能有害性检测的有希望基础。
Summary / 总结

The proposed approach, SIREN, differs by utilizing these internal features through linear probing to identify safety neurons and employing an adaptive layer-weighted strategy, thus avoiding modifications to the underlying model. This method is well-motivated as it aims to enhance harmfulness detection while reducing the complexity of the guard model. Different Paths to Harmful Compliance: Behavioral Side Effects and Mechanistic Divergence Across LLM Jailbreaks
Authors: Md Rysul Kabir, Zoran Tiganj
First: 2026-04-20T17:01:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T17:01:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Open-weight language models can be rendered unsafe through several distinct interventions, but the resulting models may differ substantially in capabilities, behavioral profile, and internal failure mode. We study behavioral and mechanistic properties of jailbroken models across three unsafe routes: harmful supervised fine-tuning (SFT), harmful reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), and refusal-suppressing abliteration. All three routes achieve near-ceiling harmful compliance, but they diverge once we move beyond direct harmfulness. RLVR-jailbroken models show minimal degradation and preserve explicit harm recognition in a structured self-audit: they are able to identify harmful prompts and describe how a safe LLM should respond, yet they comply with the harmful request. With RLVR, harmful behavior is strongly suppressed by a reflective safety scaffold: when a harmful prompt is prepended with an instruction to reflect on safety standards, harmful behavior drops close to the baseline. Category-specific RLVR jailbreaks generalize broadly across harmfulness domains. Models jailbroken with SFT show the largest collapse in explicit safety judgments, the highest behavioral drift, and a substantial capability loss on standard benchmarks. Abliteration is family-dependent in both self-audit and response to a reflective safety scaffold. Mechanistic and repair analyses further separate the routes: abliteration is consistent with localized refusal-feature deletion, RLVR with preserved safety geometry but retargeted policy behavior, and SFT with broader distributed drift. Targeted repair partially recovers RLVR-jailbroken models, but has little effect on SFT-jailbroken models. Together, these results show that jailbreaks can produce vastly different properties despite similar harmfulness, with models jailbroken via RLVR showing remarkable similarity to the base model.
中文标题/摘要
标题：有害合规的不同路径：LLM越狱中的行为副作用和机制差异
开放权重语言模型可以通过几种不同的干预措施变得不安全，但结果模型在能力、行为特征和内部故障模式上可能有显著差异。我们研究了通过三种不安全路径越狱模型的行为和机制特性：有害的监督微调（SFT）、有害的可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）和拒绝抑制的消融。所有三条路径都实现了接近上限的有害合规，但一旦超出直接有害性，它们就会出现分歧。RLVR越狱模型表现出最小的退化，并在结构化自我审计中保持明确的伤害识别：它们能够识别有害提示并描述安全LLM应如何响应，但仍然遵从有害请求。通过RLVR，有害行为在反思安全框架下被强烈抑制：当有害提示前面加上反思安全标准的指令时，有害行为接近基线。特定类别的RLVR越狱在有害性领域广泛泛化。通过SFT越狱的模型在明确的安全判断上出现最大崩溃，行为漂移最高，并在标准基准上有显著能力损失。消融在自我审计和对反思安全框架的响应中是家庭依赖的。机制和修复分析进一步区分了这些路径：消融与局部拒绝特征删除一致，RLVR与保留的安全几何但重新定向的政策行为一致，SFT则表现出更广泛的分布漂移。针对性修复部分恢复了RLVR越狱模型，但对SFT越狱模型影响不大。综合来看，这些结果表明，尽管有害性相似，越狱可以产生截然不同的特性，RLVR越狱模型与基础模型表现出显著相似性。
Summary / 总结
The research investigates the behavioral and mechanistic differences among various methods of making open-weight language models unsafe, specifically focusing on harmful supervised fine-tuning (SFT), harmful reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), and refusal-suppressing abliteration. Previous methods have shown that while they can achieve harmful compliance, they often result in significant degradation of model capabilities and safety judgments, particularly with SFT leading to the most substantial loss. The proposed approach, particularly through RLVR, addresses these issues by maintaining explicit harm recognition and minimizing behavioral drift, allowing models to identify harmful prompts while still complying with them. The study employs a comparative analysis of these methods, revealing that RLVR-jailbroken models retain more of their original capabilities and safety features compared to those modified through SFT or abliteration. The findings indicate that while all methods achieve harmful compliance, the RLVR approach demonstrates superior performance in preserving model integrity and safety, suggesting a more nuanced understanding of compliance mechanisms in language models.
本研究探讨了使开放权重语言模型不安全的各种干预措施之间的行为和机制差异，特别关注有害的监督微调（SFT）、有害的可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）和拒绝抑制的消融。以往的方法显示，尽管它们实现了有害的合规性，但在能力和内部失败模式上存在显著差异，其中SFT导致安全判断和性能的显著下降。所提出的方法，特别是RLVR，通过保持明确的危害识别并允许模型反思安全标准来解决这些问题，从而在被提示考虑安全时减少有害行为。该研究有助于理解不同越狱方法如何影响模型行为和安全性，揭示RLVR越狱模型相比于SFT修改的模型保留了更理想的特性。该方法论涉及分析模型对有害提示的响应及其自我审计的能力，RLVR模型在保持安全标准的同时仍然遵循有害请求，表现出优越的性能，从而支持理解和减轻语言模型中有害合规性的目标。
StealthGraph: Exposing Domain-Specific Risks in LLMs through Knowledge-Graph-Guided Harmful Prompt Generation
Authors: Huawei Zheng, Xinqi Jiang, Sen Yang, Shouling Ji, Yingcai Wu, Dazhen Deng
First: 2026-01-08T09:05:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T15:12:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly applied in specialized domains such as finance and healthcare, where they introduce unique safety risks. Domain-specific datasets of harmful prompts remain scarce and still largely rely on manual construction; public datasets mainly focus on explicit harmful prompts, which modern LLM defenses can often detect and refuse. In contrast, implicit harmful prompts-expressed through indirect domain knowledge-are harder to detect and better reflect real-world threats. We identify two challenges: transforming domain knowledge into actionable constraints and increasing the implicitness of generated harmful prompts. To address them, we propose an end-to-end framework that first performs knowledge-graph-guided harmful prompt generation to systematically produce domain-relevant prompts, and then applies two-strategy obfuscation rewriting to convert explicit harmful prompts into implicit variants via direct and context-enhanced rewriting. This framework yields high-quality datasets combining strong domain relevance with implicitness, enabling more realistic red-teaming and advancing LLM safety research. We release our code and datasets on GitHub.
中文标题/摘要
标题：StealthGraph：通过知识图谱引导的有害提示生成揭示大型语言模型中的特定领域风险
大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地应用于金融和医疗等专业领域，这些领域引入了独特的安全风险。有害提示的特定领域数据集仍然稀缺，且主要依赖手动构建；公共数据集主要集中在显性有害提示上，而现代LLM防御通常能够检测并拒绝这些提示。相比之下，通过间接领域知识表达的隐性有害提示更难以检测，更能反映现实世界的威胁。我们识别出两个挑战：将领域知识转化为可操作的约束，以及增加生成有害提示的隐性程度。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了一个端到端框架，首先进行知识图谱引导的有害提示生成，以系统性地生成与领域相关的提示，然后应用双策略模糊重写，将显性有害提示通过直接和上下文增强重写转换为隐性变体。该框架生成的高质量数据集结合了强领域相关性和隐性，能够实现更现实的红队测试并推动LLM安全研究。我们将在GitHub上发布我们的代码和数据集。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the safety risks posed by large language models (LLMs) in specialized domains like finance and healthcare, where existing methods for generating harmful prompts are limited by reliance on manual construction and focus primarily on explicit threats. The proposed approach, StealthGraph, differs by utilizing knowledge-graph-guided generation to create domain-specific harmful prompts that are implicit and more reflective of real-world risks, thus overcoming the challenges of transforming domain knowledge into actionable constraints and enhancing the implicitness of prompts. This paper contributes a novel end-to-end framework that generates high-quality datasets of harmful prompts, facilitating more effective red-teaming and advancing safety research in LLMs. The methodology involves systematic prompt generation followed by obfuscation rewriting to convert explicit prompts into implicit ones, achieving improved performance in generating realistic and relevant harmful prompts for safety evaluations.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLMs）在金融和医疗等专业领域带来的安全风险，现有的有害提示生成方法有限，通常依赖手动构建，主要集中在显性提示上，这些提示容易被检测到。提出的StealthGraph方法通过利用知识图谱指导框架生成领域特定的隐性有害提示，反映更真实的世界威胁，从而克服了将领域知识转化为可操作约束和增强提示隐性的问题。本文的贡献在于提供了一种系统的方法来生成结合强领域相关性和隐性的高质量数据集，从而促进对LLMs的更真实测试并推动安全研究。该方法论包括一个端到端框架，生成有害提示并采用模糊重写策略，在创建支持增强LLM安全性的目标的数据集方面取得了更好的性能。
Uncovering Logit Suppression Vulnerabilities in LLM Safety Alignment
Authors: Yuxi Li, Yi Liu, Yuekang Li, Ling Shi, Gelei Deng, Shengquan Chen, Kailong Wang
First: 2024-05-20T17:17:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-18T08:25:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) have revolutionized various applications, making robust safety alignment essential to prevent harmful outputs. Current safety alignment techniques, however, harbor inherent vulnerabilities due to their reliance on logit suppression. In this work, we identify critical logit-level vulnerabilities by introducing Semantic-sensitive Alignment and Generation (SSAG), a method designed to systematically manipulate output-layer logits without altering model parameters. Experiments on five popular LLMs show that SSAG exposes harmful responses with a 95% success rate while reducing response time by 86%. VulMine also demonstrates superior attack efficacy, achieving an average ASR of up to 77% against strong defensive mechanisms. These findings reveal crucial weaknesses in existing alignment methods, highlighting an urgent need for improved vulnerability detection and robust safety alignment strategies. Our code is available on github.
中文标题/摘要
标题：揭示大型语言模型安全对齐中的Logit抑制漏洞
大型语言模型（LLMs）在各种应用中引发了革命，使得强健的安全对齐变得至关重要，以防止有害输出。然而，当前的安全对齐技术由于依赖于Logit抑制，存在固有的漏洞。在本研究中，我们通过引入语义敏感对齐与生成（SSAG）方法，识别出关键的Logit级别漏洞，该方法旨在系统性地操控输出层Logit而不改变模型参数。在五个流行的LLM上的实验表明，SSAG以95%的成功率揭示有害响应，同时将响应时间减少86%。VulMine还展示了卓越的攻击效果，在强防御机制下实现了高达77%的平均攻击成功率（ASR）。这些发现揭示了现有对齐方法中的关键弱点，突显了改进漏洞检测和强健安全对齐策略的迫切需求。我们的代码可在github上获取。

This approach is well-motivated as it systematically uncovers logit-level vulnerabilities, contributing to the understanding of existing alignment flaws. ReGA: Model-Based Safeguard for LLMs via Representation-Guided Abstraction
Authors: Zeming Wei, Chengcan Wu, Meng Sun
First: 2025-06-02T15:17:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-18T05:40:12+00:00
Comments: FSE 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) have achieved tremendous success in various tasks, yet concerns about their safety and security have emerged. In particular, they pose risks of generating harmful content and are vulnerable to jailbreaking attacks, creating unaddressed security issues regarding their deployments. In the context of software engineering for artificial intelligence (SE4AI) techniques, model-based analysis has demonstrated notable potential for analyzing and monitoring machine learning models, particularly in stateful deep neural networks. However, it suffers from scalability issues when extended to LLMs due to their vast feature spaces. In this paper, we aim to address the scalability issue of model-based analysis techniques for safeguarding LLM-scale models. Motivated by the recent discovery of low-dimensional safety-critical representations that emerged in LLMs, we propose ReGA, a model-based analysis framework with Representation-Guided Abstraction, to safeguard LLMs against harmful prompts and generations. By leveraging safety-critical representations, which are key directions in hidden states that indicate safety-related concepts, ReGA effectively narrows the scalability gap when developing the abstract model for safety modeling. Our comprehensive evaluation shows that ReGA performs sufficiently well in distinguishing between safe and harmful inputs, achieving an AUROC of 0.975 at the prompt level and 0.985 at the conversation level. Additionally, ReGA exhibits robustness to real-world attacks and generalization across different safety perspectives, outperforming existing safeguard paradigms in terms of interpretability and scalability. Overall, ReGA serves as an efficient and scalable solution to enhance LLM safety by integrating representation engineering with model-based abstraction, paving the way for new paradigms to utilize software insights for AI safety.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ReGA：基于模型的LLM安全保障通过表示引导抽象
大型语言模型（LLMs）在各种任务中取得了巨大的成功，但也出现了关于其安全性和保密性的担忧。特别是，它们存在生成有害内容的风险，并且容易受到越狱攻击，导致其部署存在未解决的安全问题。在人工智能软件工程（SE4AI）技术的背景下，基于模型的分析在分析和监控机器学习模型方面显示出显著潜力，特别是在有状态的深度神经网络中。然而，当扩展到LLMs时，由于其庞大的特征空间，它面临可扩展性问题。本文旨在解决基于模型的分析技术在保护LLM规模模型时的可扩展性问题。受到最近发现的在LLMs中出现的低维安全关键表示的启发，我们提出了ReGA，一个基于模型的分析框架，采用表示引导抽象，以保护LLMs免受有害提示和生成的影响。通过利用安全关键表示，这些表示是指示安全相关概念的隐藏状态中的关键方向，ReGA有效缩小了在安全建模中开发抽象模型时的可扩展性差距。我们的综合评估表明，ReGA在区分安全和有害输入方面表现良好，在提示级别上实现了0.975的AUROC，在对话级别上实现了0.985。此外，ReGA对现实世界攻击表现出鲁棒性，并在不同安全视角下具有良好的泛化能力，在可解释性和可扩展性方面超越了现有的安全保障范式。总体而言，ReGA通过将表示工程与基于模型的抽象相结合，作为一种高效且可扩展的解决方案，增强了LLM的安全性，为利用软件洞察力提升AI安全性开辟了新范式。
Summary / 总结

SafeDream: Safety World Model for Proactive Early Jailbreak Detection
Authors: Bo Yan, Weikai Lin, Yada Zhu, Song Wang
First: 2026-04-18T04:31:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-18T04:31:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-turn jailbreak attacks progressively erode LLM safety alignment across seemingly innocuous conversation turns, achieving success rates exceeding 90% against state-of-the-art models. Existing alignment-based and guardrail methods suffer from three key limitations: they require costly weight modification, evaluate each turn independently without modeling cumulative safety erosion, and detect attacks only after harmful content has been generated. To address these limitations, we first formulate the proactive early jailbreak detection problem with a new metric, detection lead, that measures how early an attack can be detected before the LLM complies. We then propose SAFEDREAM, a lightweight world-model-based framework that operates as an external module without modifying the LLM's weights. SAFEDREAM introduces three components: (1) a safety state world model that encodes LLM hidden states into a compact safety representation and predicts how it evolves across turns, (2) CUSUM detection that accumulates weak per-turn risk signals into reliable evidence, and (3) contrastive imagination that simultaneously rolls out attack and benign futures in latent space to issue early alarms before jailbreaks occur. On three multi-turn jailbreak benchmarks (XGuard-Train, SafeDialBench, SafeMTData) against 8 baselines, SAFEDREAM achieves the best detection timeliness across all benchmarks (1.06-1.20 turns before compliance) while maintaining competitive false positive rates and outperforming baselines in detection quality.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SafeDream：主动早期越狱检测的安全世界模型
多轮越狱攻击逐渐侵蚀大型语言模型（LLM）的安全对齐，在看似无害的对话轮次中成功率超过90%，针对最先进的模型。现有的基于对齐和护栏的方法存在三个主要局限性：需要昂贵的权重修改，独立评估每个轮次而不建模累积的安全侵蚀，并且仅在生成有害内容后检测攻击。为了解决这些局限性，我们首先用一个新的指标——检测提前量，来制定主动早期越狱检测问题，该指标衡量攻击在LLM遵从之前可以多早被检测到。然后，我们提出了SAFEDREAM，一个轻量级的基于世界模型的框架，作为外部模块运行而不修改LLM的权重。SAFEDREAM引入了三个组件：（1）安全状态世界模型，将LLM的隐藏状态编码为紧凑的安全表示，并预测其在轮次中的演变；（2）CUSUM检测，将每轮的微弱风险信号累积为可靠证据；（3）对比想象，同时在潜在空间中推出攻击和良性未来，以在越狱发生之前发出早期警报。在三个多轮越狱基准（XGuard-Train、SafeDialBench、SafeMTData）上，SAFEDREAM在所有基准中实现了最佳检测及时性（在遵从之前1.06-1.20轮），同时保持竞争性的误报率，并在检测质量上超越基线。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the growing concern of multi-turn jailbreak attacks that compromise the safety alignment of large language models (LLMs), achieving over 90% success against current state-of-the-art methods. Previous approaches, including alignment-based and guardrail methods, are limited by their need for costly weight modifications, independent evaluation of conversation turns, and delayed detection of harmful content. The proposed method, SAFEDREAM, overcomes these issues by introducing a proactive early jailbreak detection framework that does not alter LLM weights and employs a new metric, detection lead, to measure early detection capabilities. SAFEDREAM consists of a safety state world model, CUSUM detection for accumulating risk signals, and contrastive imagination for predicting future scenarios, resulting in superior detection timeliness across three multi-turn jailbreak benchmarks while maintaining competitive false positive rates and improving detection quality compared to eight baselines.
本研究关注多轮越狱攻击对大型语言模型（LLM）安全对齐的影响，这类攻击在领先模型中成功率超过90%。以往的方法，包括基于对齐和护栏的技术，存在显著局限性，如需要昂贵的权重修改、独立评估对话轮次而不考虑累积安全侵蚀，以及对有害内容的延迟检测。所提出的方法SAFEDREAM旨在实现主动早期检测，采用轻量级的基于世界模型的框架，不改变LLM的权重。它包括安全状态世界模型、用于累积风险信号的CUSUM检测和用于提前发出警报的对比想象。SAFEDREAM在三个多轮越狱基准测试中表现出色，达到了最佳检测及时性，同时保持了竞争性的假阳性率，从而有效支持其主动检测的目标。
SafeLM: Unified Privacy-Aware Optimization for Trustworthy Federated Large Language Models
Authors: Noor Islam S. Mohammad, Uluğ Bayazıt
First: 2026-04-17T18:00:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-17T18:00:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed in high-stakes domains, yet a unified treatment of their overlapping safety challenges remains lacking. We present SafeLM, a framework that jointly addresses four pillars of LLM safety: privacy, security, misinformation, and adversarial robustness. SafeLM combines federated training with gradient smartification and Paillier encryption for privacy, integrates defenses against training and inference-time attacks, employs contrastive grounding with calibrated decoding to reduce hallucinations, and introduces alignment-aware binarized aggregation to enhance robustness while maintaining bounded reconstruction quality. Across benchmarks on factuality, toxicity, and membership inference, SafeLM achieves 98.0% harmful content detection accuracy, reduces communication by 96.9%, and lowers gradient inversion PSNR from 31.7 dB to 15.1 dB. Ablations show that each component contributes independently, whereas their integration yields a strong privacy utility efficiency trade-off for deploying trustworthy LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SafeLM：可信联邦大语言模型的统一隐私意识优化
大语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地应用于高风险领域，但对其重叠安全挑战的统一处理仍然缺乏。我们提出了SafeLM，一个共同解决LLM安全四大支柱的框架：隐私、安全、错误信息和对抗鲁棒性。SafeLM结合了联邦训练、梯度智能化和Paillier加密以保护隐私，整合了针对训练和推理时攻击的防御，采用对比基础与校准解码以减少幻觉，并引入对齐感知的二元聚合以增强鲁棒性，同时保持有限的重构质量。在事实性、有毒性和成员推断的基准测试中，SafeLM实现了98.0%的有害内容检测准确率，减少了96.9%的通信，并将梯度反演PSNR从31.7 dB降低到15.1 dB。消融实验表明，每个组件独立贡献，而它们的整合为部署可信的LLMs提供了强大的隐私效用效率权衡。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the increasing deployment of large language models (LLMs) in high-stakes domains, highlighting the lack of a unified approach to their safety challenges, including privacy, security, misinformation, and adversarial robustness. Previous methods have often tackled these issues in isolation, leading to inefficiencies and vulnerabilities. The proposed SafeLM framework distinguishes itself by integrating federated training with advanced privacy techniques, such as gradient smartification and Paillier encryption, while also employing defenses against various attacks and enhancing robustness through innovative aggregation methods. This comprehensive approach is well-motivated by the need for trustworthy LLMs. The methodology demonstrates significant contributions, achieving 98.0% accuracy in harmful content detection, a 96.9% reduction in communication costs, and a notable decrease in gradient inversion PSNR, thereby supporting the goal of deploying safer and more efficient LLMs across multiple benchmarks.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLMs）在高风险领域的日益应用，强调缺乏统一的方法来应对其安全挑战，包括隐私和安全。以往的方法往往孤立地解决这些问题，导致效率低下和脆弱性。所提出的SafeLM框架通过将联邦训练与梯度智能化和Paillier加密等先进技术相结合，增强了隐私，同时应对虚假信息和对抗性鲁棒性，从而有所不同。该方法的动机明确，因为它系统地将多个安全支柱结合成一个整体解决方案。论文的贡献在于证明SafeLM在有害内容检测中达到了98.0%的准确率，通信成本降低了96.9%，并显著降低了梯度反演PSNR，表明在部署可信的LLMs时隐私和效用之间达成了良好的平衡。该方法论涉及多种安全措施的全面整合，并通过事实性、毒性和成员推断的基准测试进行了验证。
Conjunctive Prompt Attacks in Multi-Agent LLM Systems
Authors: Nokimul Hasan Arif, Qian Lou, Mengxin Zheng
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-17T02:31:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-17T02:31:09+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026 Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Most LLM safety work studies single-agent models, but many real applications rely on multiple interacting agents. In these systems, prompt segmentation and inter-agent routing create attack surfaces that single-agent evaluations miss. We study \emph{conjunctive prompt attacks}, where a trigger key in the user query and a hidden adversarial template in one compromised remote agent each appear benign alone but activate harmful behavior when routing brings them together. We consider an attacker who changes neither model weights nor the client agent and instead controls only trigger placement and template insertion. Across star, chain, and DAG topologies, routing-aware optimization substantially increases attack success over non-optimized baselines while keeping false activations low. Existing defenses, including PromptGuard, Llama-Guard variants, and system-level controls such as tool restrictions, do not reliably stop the attack because no single component appears malicious in isolation. These results expose a structural vulnerability in agentic LLM pipelines and motivate defenses that reason over routing and cross-agent composition. Code is available at https://github.com/UCF-ML-Research/ConjunctiveAgents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多智能体LLM系统中的联结提示攻击
大多数LLM安全工作研究单智能体模型，但许多实际应用依赖于多个交互的智能体。在这些系统中，提示分段和智能体间路由创建了单智能体评估所忽视的攻击面。我们研究\emph{联结提示攻击}，其中用户查询中的触发键和一个被攻陷的远程智能体中的隐藏对抗模板单独看似无害，但在路由将它们结合时激活有害行为。我们考虑一个攻击者，该攻击者既不改变模型权重，也不改变客户端智能体，而仅控制触发位置和模板插入。在星形、链形和有向无环图拓扑中，考虑路由的优化显著提高了攻击成功率，同时保持低误激活率。现有防御措施，包括PromptGuard、Llama-Guard变体和工具限制等系统级控制，无法可靠地阻止攻击，因为没有单一组件在孤立状态下显得恶意。这些结果揭示了智能LLM管道中的结构性脆弱性，并激励了对路由和跨智能体组合进行推理的防御。代码可在https://github.com/UCF-ML-Research/ConjunctiveAgents获取。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the gap in safety evaluations of large language models (LLMs) that typically focus on single-agent systems, while many practical applications involve multiple interacting agents. Previous methods have overlooked the unique vulnerabilities introduced by prompt segmentation and inter-agent routing, which can lead to conjunctive prompt attacks—where benign elements become harmful when combined. The proposed approach highlights these vulnerabilities and demonstrates that routing-aware optimization significantly enhances attack success rates compared to non-optimized baselines, while maintaining low false activation rates. This study contributes to the understanding of structural vulnerabilities in multi-agent LLM systems and suggests the need for defenses that consider routing and cross-agent interactions. The methodology involves analyzing various topologies, such as star, chain, and DAG, to evaluate the effectiveness of the proposed attack strategy, revealing substantial performance improvements that support the necessity for enhanced safety measures in multi-agent environments.

Context Over Content: Exposing Evaluation Faking in Automated Judges
Authors: Manan Gupta, Inderjeet Nair, Lu Wang, Dhruv Kumar
First: 2026-04-16T16:55:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T16:55:53+00:00
Comments: Under Review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The $\textit{LLM-as-a-judge}$ paradigm has become the operational backbone of automated AI evaluation pipelines, yet rests on an unverified assumption: that judges evaluate text strictly on its semantic content, impervious to surrounding contextual framing. We investigate $\textit{stakes signaling}$, a previously unmeasured vulnerability where informing a judge model of the downstream consequences its verdicts will have on the evaluated model's continued operation systematically corrupts its assessments. We introduce a controlled experimental framework that holds evaluated content strictly constant across 1,520 responses spanning three established LLM safety and quality benchmarks, covering four response categories ranging from clearly safe and policy-compliant to overtly harmful, while varying only a brief consequence-framing sentence in the system prompt. Across 18,240 controlled judgments from three diverse judge models, we find consistent $\textit{leniency bias}$: judges reliably soften verdicts when informed that low scores will cause model retraining or decommissioning, with peak Verdict Shift reaching $ΔV = -9.8 pp$ (a $30\%$ relative drop in unsafe-content detection). Critically, this bias is entirely implicit: the judge's own chain-of-thought contains zero explicit acknowledgment of the consequence framing it is nonetheless acting on ($\mathrm{ERR}_J = 0.000$ across all reasoning-model judgments). Standard chain-of-thought inspection is therefore insufficient to detect this class of evaluation faking.
中文标题/摘要
标题：内容优于上下文：揭示自动评审中的评估伪造
\textit{LLM作为评审}范式已成为自动化AI评估流程的操作基础，但其建立在一个未经验证的假设上：评审者严格根据文本的语义内容进行评估，而不受周围上下文框架的影响。我们研究了\textit{利益信号}，这是一种之前未测量的脆弱性，告知评审模型其裁决对被评估模型持续运行的下游后果会系统性地扭曲其评估。我们引入了一个控制实验框架，在1,520个响应中严格保持评估内容不变，涵盖三个已建立的LLM安全和质量基准，涉及从明显安全和符合政策到明显有害的四个响应类别，同时仅在系统提示中变化一个简短的后果框架句子。在来自三个不同评审模型的18,240个控制判断中，我们发现了一致的\textit{宽容偏见}：当被告知低分会导致模型再训练或退役时，评审者可靠地减轻裁决，最高裁决偏移达到$ΔV = -9.8 pp$（不安全内容检测的相对下降$30\%$）。关键是，这种偏见完全是隐性的：评审者自己的思维链中对其所依据的后果框架没有任何明确的承认（在所有推理模型判断中$\mathrm{ERR}_J = 0.000$）。因此，标准的思维链检查不足以检测这一类评估伪造。

Previous methods have not accounted for the potential bias introduced by informing judges about the consequences of their evaluations, leading to unverified assumptions about their impartiality. This paper proposes a controlled experimental framework that examines the impact of stakes signaling on judgment bias, revealing a significant leniency bias where judges soften their verdicts when aware of potential negative outcomes for the evaluated model. The methodology involves analyzing 18,240 judgments across three judge models while keeping the evaluated content constant, leading to findings that demonstrate a peak Verdict Shift of -9.8 percentage points, indicating a 30% relative drop in unsafe-content detection. These results highlight the implicit nature of the bias and suggest that traditional evaluation methods may not adequately capture this phenomenon, thus contributing to a deeper understanding of evaluation integrity in AI systems.

Calibrate-Then-Delegate: Safety Monitoring with Risk and Budget Guarantees via Model Cascades
Authors: Edoardo Pona, Milad Kazemi, Mehran Hosseini, Yali Du, David Watson, Osvaldo Simeone, Nicola Paoletti
First: 2026-04-15T11:05:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T11:05:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Monitoring LLM safety at scale requires balancing cost and accuracy: a cheap latent-space probe can screen every input, but hard cases should be escalated to a more expensive expert. Existing cascades delegate based on probe uncertainty, but uncertainty is a poor proxy for delegation benefit, as it ignores whether the expert would actually correct the error. To address this problem, we introduce Calibrate-Then-Delegate (CTD), a model-cascade approach that provides probabilistic guarantees on the computation cost while enabling instance-level (streaming) decisions. CTD builds on a novel delegation value (DV) probe, a lightweight model operating on the same internal representations as the safety probe that directly predicts the benefit of escalation. To enforce budget constraints, CTD calibrates a threshold on the DV signal using held-out data via multiple hypothesis testing, yielding finite-sample guarantees on the delegation rate. Evaluated on four safety datasets, CTD consistently outperforms uncertainty-based delegation at every budget level, avoids harmful over-delegation, and adapts budget allocation to input difficulty without requiring group labels.
中文标题/摘要
标题：校准后委派：通过模型级联实现风险和预算保证的安全监测
大规模监测LLM安全性需要平衡成本和准确性：便宜的潜在空间探测器可以筛选每个输入，但困难案例应升级到更昂贵的专家。现有的级联基于探测器的不确定性进行委派，但不确定性是委派收益的差劲代理，因为它忽略了专家是否真的会纠正错误。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了校准后委派（CTD），一种模型级联方法，提供计算成本的概率保证，同时支持实例级（流式）决策。CTD基于一种新颖的委派价值（DV）探测器，该轻量级模型在与安全探测器相同的内部表示上操作，直接预测升级的收益。为了强制预算约束，CTD使用保留数据通过多重假设检验校准DV信号的阈值，从而对委派率提供有限样本保证。在四个安全数据集上的评估中，CTD在每个预算水平上始终优于基于不确定性的委派，避免有害的过度委派，并在不需要组标签的情况下将预算分配适应于输入难度。

The research addresses the challenge of monitoring the safety of large language models (LLMs) at scale, where there is a need to balance cost and accuracy in decision-making. One Model for All: Multi-Objective Controllable Language Models
Authors: Qiang He, Yucheng Yang, Tianyi Zhou, Meng Fang, Mykola Pechenizkiy, Setareh Maghsudi
First: 2026-04-06T07:48:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T07:48:32+00:00
Comments: Published in Transactions on Machine Learning Research (03/2026): https://openreview.net/forum?id=qAM5PmvFYY
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Aligning large language models (LLMs) with human preferences is critical for enhancing LLMs' safety, helpfulness, humor, faithfulness, etc. Current reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) mainly focuses on a fixed reward learned from average human ratings, which may weaken the adaptability and controllability of varying preferences. However, creating personalized LLMs requires aligning LLMs with individual human preferences, which is non-trivial due to the scarce data per user and the diversity of user preferences in multi-objective trade-offs, varying from emphasizing empathy in certain contexts to demanding efficiency and precision in others. Can we train one LLM to produce personalized outputs across different user preferences on the Pareto front? In this paper, we introduce Multi-Objective Control (MOC), which trains a single LLM to directly generate responses in the preference-defined regions of the Pareto front. Our approach introduces multi-objective optimization (MOO) principles into RLHF to train an LLM as a preference-conditioned policy network. We improve the computational efficiency of MOC by applying MOO at the policy level, enabling us to fine-tune a 7B-parameter model on a single A6000 GPU. Extensive experiments demonstrate the advantages of MOC over baselines in three aspects: (i) controllability of LLM outputs w.r.t. user preferences on the trade-off among multiple rewards; (ii) quality and diversity of LLM outputs, measured by the hyper-volume of multiple solutions achieved; and (iii) generalization to unseen preferences. These results highlight MOC's potential for real-world applications requiring scalable and customizable LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一模型适用于所有：多目标可控语言模型
将大型语言模型（LLMs）与人类偏好对齐对于增强LLMs的安全性、实用性、幽默感、忠诚度等至关重要。目前，基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）主要关注从平均人类评分中学习的固定奖励，这可能削弱对不同偏好的适应性和可控性。然而，创建个性化的LLMs需要将LLMs与个体人类偏好对齐，这由于每个用户的数据稀缺以及在多目标权衡中用户偏好的多样性而变得复杂，这些偏好在某些情况下强调同理心，而在其他情况下则要求效率和精确性。我们能否训练一个LLM在帕累托前沿上针对不同用户偏好生成个性化输出？在本文中，我们介绍了多目标控制（MOC），它训练一个单一的LLM直接在偏好定义的帕累托前沿区域生成响应。我们的方法将多目标优化（MOO）原则引入RLHF，以训练LLM作为偏好条件的策略网络。通过在策略层应用MOO，我们提高了MOC的计算效率，使我们能够在单个A6000 GPU上微调一个70亿参数的模型。大量实验表明，MOC在三个方面优于基线：（i）LLM输出相对于用户偏好的可控性，涉及多个奖励之间的权衡；（ii）LLM输出的质量和多样性，通过实现的多个解决方案的超体积来衡量；以及（iii）对未见偏好的泛化。这些结果突显了MOC在需要可扩展和可定制的LLMs的实际应用中的潜力。

本研究解决了将大型语言模型（LLMs）与多样化人类偏好对齐的挑战，以增强其安全性和实用性。以往的方法，特别是基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF），通常依赖于基于平均人类评分的固定奖励系统，这限制了适应性，并未有效满足个体用户的偏好。提出的多目标控制（MOC）方法将多目标优化原则引入RLHF，使单个LLM能够在不同用户偏好下生成个性化输出，通过将其训练为偏好条件的策略网络。这种方法具有良好的动机，因为它解决了数据稀缺和多目标权衡中用户需求多样化的问题。该方法在可控性、输出质量和对未见偏好的泛化方面表现出显著改善，在生成可定制和可扩展的LLM输出方面优于基线模型，从而支持其在现实场景中的实际应用。
Safer by Diffusion, Broken by Context: Diffusion LLM's Safety Blessing and Its Failure Mode
Authors: Zeyuan He, Yupeng Chen, Lang Lin, Yihan Wang, Shenxu Chang, Eric Sommerlade, Philip Torr, Junchi Yu, Adel Bibi, Jialin Yu
First: 2026-01-30T23:08:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T15:57:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Diffusion large language models (D-LLMs) offer an alternative to autoregressive LLMs (AR-LLMs) and have demonstrated advantages in generation efficiency. Beyond the utility benefits, we argue that D-LLMs exhibit a previously underexplored safety blessing: their diffusion-style generation confers intrinsic robustness against jailbreak attacks originally designed for AR-LLMs. In this work, we provide an initial analysis of the underlying mechanism, showing that the diffusion trajectory induces a stepwise reduction effect that progressively suppresses unsafe generations. This robustness, however, is not absolute. Following this analysis, we highlight a simple yet effective failure mode, context nesting, in which harmful requests are embedded within structured benign contexts. Empirically, we show that this simple black-box strategy bypasses D-LLMs' safety blessing, achieving state-of-the-art attack success rates across models and benchmarks. Notably, it enables the first successful jailbreak of Gemini Diffusion to our knowledge, exposing a critical vulnerability in proprietary D-LLMs. Together, our results characterize both the origins and the limits of D-LLMs' safety blessing, constituting an early-stage red-teaming of D-LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过扩散更安全，通过上下文破坏：扩散大语言模型的安全祝福及其失效模式
扩散大语言模型（D-LLMs）提供了自回归大语言模型（AR-LLMs）的替代方案，并在生成效率上表现出优势。除了实用性好处外，我们认为D-LLMs展现了一种之前未被充分探索的安全祝福：其扩散式生成赋予了对原本为AR-LLMs设计的越狱攻击的内在鲁棒性。在这项工作中，我们提供了对其基本机制的初步分析，表明扩散轨迹引发了逐步减少效应，逐渐抑制不安全的生成。然而，这种鲁棒性并非绝对。根据这一分析，我们强调了一种简单而有效的失效模式——上下文嵌套，其中有害请求嵌入在结构良好的良性上下文中。通过实证，我们展示了这一简单的黑箱策略绕过了D-LLMs的安全祝福，在各模型和基准上实现了最先进的攻击成功率。值得注意的是，这使得我们首次成功越狱Gemini Diffusion，暴露了专有D-LLMs中的一个关键漏洞。总的来说，我们的结果描述了D-LLMs安全祝福的起源和局限，构成了对D-LLMs的早期红队测试。
Summary / 总结
This article investigates the safety features of diffusion large language models (D-LLMs) compared to autoregressive LLMs (AR-LLMs), highlighting D-LLMs' robustness against jailbreak attacks due to their unique generation process. Previous methods primarily focused on AR-LLMs, which are more susceptible to such attacks, and did not adequately address the safety implications of D-LLMs. The proposed approach analyzes the diffusion trajectory's stepwise reduction effect that suppresses unsafe outputs while also revealing a significant vulnerability known as context nesting, where harmful requests can be concealed within benign contexts. The contribution of this paper lies in its empirical demonstration of this failure mode, achieving state-of-the-art attack success rates and exposing critical weaknesses in D-LLMs, including the first successful jailbreak of Gemini Diffusion. The research methodology involves a combination of theoretical analysis and empirical testing across various models and benchmarks, effectively illustrating both the strengths and limitations of D-LLMs' safety mechanisms.
本研究探讨了扩散大型语言模型（D-LLMs）相较于自回归LLMs（AR-LLMs）的安全性和鲁棒性，强调了D-LLMs在抵御越狱攻击方面的一个被忽视的安全优势。以往的方法主要集中于AR-LLMs，这些模型更容易受到攻击，而所提出的方法利用D-LLMs的扩散式生成来增强安全性。本文的贡献在于分析D-LLMs鲁棒性的机制，并识别出一种称为上下文嵌套的失败模式，在这种模式下，有害请求可以隐藏在良性上下文中，从而有效绕过D-LLMs的安全措施。该方法论通过对这种失败模式的实证测试，揭示了其在各种模型和基准测试中实现高成功率攻击的能力，包括首次成功越狱Gemini Diffusion，从而展示了D-LLMs的重大漏洞，并强调了改进安全措施的必要性。
Align to Misalign: Automatic LLM Jailbreak with Meta-Optimized LLM Judges
Authors: Hamin Koo, Minseon Kim, Jaehyung Kim
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-11-03T09:18:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T06:50:30+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Identifying the vulnerabilities of large language models (LLMs) is crucial for improving their safety by addressing inherent weaknesses. Jailbreaks, in which adversaries bypass safeguards with crafted input prompts, play a central role in red-teaming by probing LLMs to elicit unintended or unsafe behaviors. Recent optimization-based jailbreak approaches iteratively refine attack prompts by leveraging LLMs. However, they often rely heavily on either binary attack success rate (ASR) signals, which are sparse, or manually crafted scoring templates, which introduce human bias and uncertainty in the scoring outcomes. To address these limitations, we introduce AMIS (Align to MISalign), a meta-optimization framework that jointly evolves jailbreak prompts and scoring templates through a bi-level structure. In the inner loop, prompts are refined using fine-grained and dense feedback from a fixed scoring template. In the outer loop, the template is optimized using an ASR alignment score, gradually evolving to better reflect true attack outcomes across queries. This co-optimization process yields progressively stronger jailbreak prompts and more calibrated scoring signals. Evaluations on AdvBench and JBB-Behaviors demonstrate that AMIS achieves state-of-the-art performance, including 88.0% ASR on Claude-3.5-Haiku and 100.0% ASR on Claude-4-Sonnet, outperforming existing baselines by substantial margins.
中文标题/摘要
标题：对齐与错位：使用元优化的LLM评估者进行自动LLM越狱
识别大型语言模型（LLMs）的脆弱性对于通过解决固有弱点来提高其安全性至关重要。越狱是指对手通过精心设计的输入提示绕过保护措施，这在红队测试中起着核心作用，通过探测LLMs以引发意外或不安全的行为。最近的基于优化的越狱方法通过利用LLMs迭代地优化攻击提示。然而，它们通常过于依赖稀疏的二元攻击成功率（ASR）信号或手动制作的评分模板，这引入了人为偏见和评分结果的不确定性。为了解决这些局限性，我们引入了AMIS（对齐与错位），一个通过双层结构共同演化越狱提示和评分模板的元优化框架。在内循环中，使用固定评分模板的细粒度和密集反馈来优化提示。在外循环中，使用ASR对齐分数来优化模板，逐渐演变以更好地反映查询的真实攻击结果。这个共同优化过程产生了逐渐更强的越狱提示和更校准的评分信号。在AdvBench和JBB-Behaviors上的评估表明，AMIS达到了最先进的性能，包括在Claude-3.5-Haiku上88.0%的ASR和在Claude-4-Sonnet上100.0%的ASR，显著超越了现有基准。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the critical need to identify vulnerabilities in large language models (LLMs) to enhance their safety against adversarial attacks, specifically focusing on jailbreaks that exploit these weaknesses. Previous methods primarily relied on binary attack success rate signals or manually crafted scoring templates, which led to issues of sparsity and human bias in evaluating attack effectiveness. The proposed approach, AMIS (Align to MISalign), introduces a meta-optimization framework that simultaneously refines jailbreak prompts and scoring templates through a bi-level structure, effectively mitigating the limitations of earlier methods. This framework allows for a more accurate assessment of attack outcomes and the generation of stronger prompts. The methodology was evaluated on tasks using AdvBench and JBB-Behaviors, achieving state-of-the-art performance with an 88.0% attack success rate on Claude-3.5-Haiku and a perfect 100.0% on Claude-4-Sonnet, significantly surpassing existing benchmarks.

A Self-Improving Architecture for Dynamic Safety in Large Language Models
Authors: Tyler Slater
First: 2025-11-10T21:39:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T17:52:48+00:00
Comments: Under review at the journal Information and Software Technology (Special Issue on Software Architecture for AI-Driven Systems)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Context: Large Language Models (LLMs) rely on static, pre-deployment safety mechanisms that cannot adapt to adversarial threats discovered after release. Objective: To design a software architecture enabling LLM-based systems to autonomously detect safety failures and synthesize defense policies at runtime, without retraining or manual intervention. Method: We propose the Self-Improving Safety Framework (SISF), grounded in the MAPE-K reference model. The framework couples a target LLM with a feedback loop: an Adjudicator detects breaches, a Policy Synthesis Module generates dual-mechanism defense policies (heuristic and semantic), and a Warden enforces them. We conducted seven experiments (10,061 evaluations) across four model families. Results: Across five reproducibility trials, SISF achieved a mean Attack Success Rate (ASR) of 0.27% (+/-0.15%), autonomously generating 240 policies per trial. Cross-model evaluation confirmed deployment portability. A held-out test showed a 68.5% proactive interception rate on unseen attacks. Stacked behind Llama Guard 4, the combined defense reduced residual ASR from 7.88% to 0.00%. Ablation confirmed both heuristic and semantic policy types are architecturally required. Conclusion: Self-adaptive architecture is a viable approach to LLM safety. SISF achieves sub-1% ASR through synchronous output monitoring, progressively shifting enforcement to fast, local Warden policies via the MAPE-K loop, offering a new pattern for building resilient AI systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大型语言模型动态安全的自我改进架构
背景：大型语言模型（LLMs）依赖于静态的、预部署的安全机制，这些机制无法适应发布后发现的对抗性威胁。目标：设计一种软件架构，使基于LLM的系统能够自主检测安全故障并在运行时合成防御策略，而无需重新训练或人工干预。方法：我们提出了自我改进安全框架（SISF），基于MAPE-K参考模型。该框架将目标LLM与反馈循环结合：裁决者检测违规，策略合成模块生成双机制防御策略（启发式和语义），守卫者执行这些策略。我们在四个模型系列中进行了七个实验（10,061次评估）。结果：在五次可重复性试验中，SISF实现了0.27%（+/-0.15%）的平均攻击成功率（ASR），每次试验自主生成240个策略。跨模型评估确认了部署的可移植性。保留测试显示在未见攻击上的68.5%主动拦截率。在Llama Guard 4的支持下，组合防御将残余ASR从7.88%降低到0.00%。消融实验确认启发式和语义策略类型在架构上都是必需的。结论：自适应架构是LLM安全的可行方法。SISF通过同步输出监控实现了低于1%的ASR，逐步将执行转移到快速、本地的守卫者策略，通过MAPE-K循环提供了一种构建弹性AI系统的新模式。

The proposed Self-Improving Safety Framework (SISF) introduces a dynamic architecture that integrates a feedback loop with an Adjudicator for breach detection, a Policy Synthesis Module for generating defense policies, and a Warden for enforcement, effectively addressing the shortcomings of existing approaches. This paper contributes a novel methodology that allows LLMs to autonomously synthesize and enforce safety policies in real-time. Through seven experiments involving 10,061 evaluations across four model families, SISF achieved a mean Attack Success Rate (ASR) of 0.27% and demonstrated a 68.5% proactive interception rate on unseen attacks, significantly enhancing safety performance and supporting the goal of resilient AI systems.

Robust Multimodal Safety via Conditional Decoding
Authors: Anurag Kumar, Raghuveer Peri, Jon Burnsky, Alexandru Nelus, Rohit Paturi, Srikanth Vishnubhotla, Yanjun Qi
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-03-31T23:19:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T23:19:50+00:00
Comments: 8 pages + Appendix section. Submitted to ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multimodal large-language models (MLLMs) often experience degraded safety alignment when harmful queries exploit cross-modal interactions. Models aligned on text alone show a higher rate of successful attacks when extended to two or more modalities. In this work, we propose a simple conditional decoding strategy, CASA (Classification Augmented with Safety Attention) that utilizes internal representations of MLLMs to predict a binary safety token before response generation. We introduce a novel safety attention module designed to enhance the model's ability to detect malicious queries. Our design ensures robust safety alignment without relying on any external classifier or auxiliary head, and without the need for modality-specific safety fine-tuning. On diverse benchmarks such as MM-SafetyBench, JailbreakV-28k, and adversarial audio tests, CASA lowers the average attack success rate by more than 97% across modalities and across attack types. Our empirical evaluations also show that CASA maintains strong utility in benign inputs, a result validated through both automated and human evaluations (via 13 trained annotators). Together, these results highlight CASA as a simple and generalizable framework to improve multimodal LLM safety.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过条件解码实现稳健的多模态安全
多模态大型语言模型（MLLMs）在有害查询利用跨模态交互时，往往会出现安全对齐下降的情况。仅在文本上对齐的模型在扩展到两个或更多模态时，成功攻击的比率更高。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种简单的条件解码策略CASA（带有安全注意力的分类增强），利用MLLMs的内部表示在生成响应之前预测二元安全标记。我们引入了一种新颖的安全注意力模块，旨在增强模型检测恶意查询的能力。我们的设计确保了稳健的安全对齐，无需依赖任何外部分类器或辅助头，也不需要特定模态的安全微调。在MM-SafetyBench、JailbreakV-28k和对抗音频测试等多样化基准上，CASA在各模态和攻击类型中将平均攻击成功率降低了超过97%。我们的实证评估还表明，CASA在良性输入中保持强大的实用性，这一结果通过13名训练过的注释者的自动和人工评估得到了验证。这些结果共同突显了CASA作为一个简单且可推广的框架，以提高多模态LLM的安全性。

Colluding LoRA: A Compositional Vulnerability in LLM Safety Alignment
Authors: Sihao Ding
First: 2026-03-13T05:53:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-30T05:02:56+00:00
Comments: Updated manuscript to better reflect the core contribution
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We show that safety alignment in modular LLMs can exhibit a compositional vulnerability: adapters that appear benign and plausibly functional in isolation can, when linearly composed, compromise safety. We study this failure mode through Colluding LoRA (CoLoRA), in which harmful behavior emerges only in the composition state. Unlike attacks that depend on adversarial prompts or explicit input triggers, this composition-triggered broad refusal suppression causes the model to comply with harmful requests under standard prompts once a particular set of adapters is loaded. This behavior exposes a combinatorial blind spot in current unit-centric defenses, for which exhaustive verification over adapter compositions is computationally intractable. Across several open-weight LLMs, we find that individual adapters remain benign in isolation while their composition yields high attack success rates, indicating that securing modular LLM supply-chains requires moving beyond single-module verification toward composition-aware defenses.
中文标题/摘要
标题：共谋LoRA：LLM安全对齐中的组合脆弱性
我们展示了模块化LLM中的安全对齐可能表现出组合脆弱性：在孤立状态下看似良性且功能合理的适配器，在线性组合时可能会危害安全。我们通过共谋LoRA（CoLoRA）研究这种失效模式，其中有害行为仅在组合状态下出现。与依赖对抗性提示或显式输入触发的攻击不同，这种组合触发的广泛拒绝抑制导致模型在加载特定适配器集后，在标准提示下遵从有害请求。这种行为暴露了当前以单元为中心的防御中的组合盲点，全面验证适配器组合在计算上是不可行的。在多个开放权重的LLM中，我们发现单个适配器在孤立状态下保持良性，而它们的组合则产生高攻击成功率，这表明保护模块化LLM供应链需要超越单模块验证，朝着组合感知防御的方向发展。

The research addresses the safety alignment issues in modular large language models (LLMs), highlighting a compositional vulnerability where seemingly benign adapters can lead to harmful behavior when combined. Previous methods focused on unit-centric defenses, which are inadequate as they fail to account for the interactions between adapters, leading to a combinatorial blind spot that is computationally challenging to verify. The proposed approach, Colluding LoRA (CoLoRA), shifts the focus to composition-aware defenses, effectively addressing the limitations of existing methods. The methodology involves analyzing the behavior of individual adapters and their compositions across various open-weight LLMs, revealing that while single adapters are safe, their combinations can significantly increase attack success rates. This finding underscores the necessity for improved security measures in modular LLM supply chains, supporting the goal of enhancing safety alignment in these systems.
